\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FillRectangularWithSpheres()}{FillRectangularWithSpheres()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$ size\+\_\+t $>$ openphase\+::\+Initializations\+::\+Fill\+Rectangular\+With\+Spheres (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1PhaseField}{Phase\+Field}} \&}]{Phase,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1BoundaryConditions}{Boundary\+Conditions}} \&}]{BC,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1Settings}{Settings}} \&}]{loc\+Settings,  }\item[{std\+::function$<$ size\+\_\+t(long int, long int, long int)$>$}]{Phase\+Index,  }\item[{double}]{Mean\+Radius,  }\item[{double}]{Std\+Radius,  }\item[{long int}]{x\+\_\+min,  }\item[{long int}]{x\+\_\+max,  }\item[{long int}]{y\+\_\+min,  }\item[{long int}]{y\+\_\+max,  }\item[{long int}]{z\+\_\+min,  }\item[{long int}]{z\+\_\+max,  }\item[{double}]{Min\+Distance,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{Random\+Seed\+Input,  }\item[{bool}]{Verbose = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Fills rectangular domain densely with spherical grains of normal distributed size. Fills rectangular domain densely with spherical grains of normal distributed size with specified relative density. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Phase\+Index} & function that determines the phases of the grain which may depend on the position (i,j,k).  \\
\hline
{\em Mean\+Radius} & Mean radius of grains  \\
\hline
{\em Std\+Radius} & Standard deviation grain radius  \\
\hline
{\em x\+\_\+min} & First x-\/index of rectangular  \\
\hline
{\em x\+\_\+max} & Last x-\/index of rectangular  \\
\hline
{\em y\+\_\+min} & First y-\/index of rectangular  \\
\hline
{\em y\+\_\+max} & Last y-\/index of rectangular  \\
\hline
{\em z\+\_\+min} & First a-\/index of rectangular  \\
\hline
{\em z\+\_\+max} & Last z-\/index of rectangular  \\
\hline
{\em Min\+Distance} & Minimal distance of grains which can be negative for even denser microstructure!  \\
\hline
{\em Random\+Seed\+Input} & Random number seed for initialization \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class T , size\+\_\+t Rank$>$ \\
static bool openphase\+::\+Initializations\+::loop\+\_\+sphere\+\_\+with\+\_\+exit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1Storage3D}{Storage3D}}$<$ T, Rank $>$ \&}]{field,  }\item[{const std\+::function$<$ bool(long int, long int, long int, double)$>$ \&}]{func,  }\item[{const double}]{x0,  }\item[{const double}]{y0,  }\item[{const double}]{z0,  }\item[{const double}]{radius,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1GridParameters}{Grid\+Parameters}} \&}]{Dimensions,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classopenphase_1_1BoundaryConditions}{Boundary\+Conditions}} \&}]{BC }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



Loops over all points (i,j,k) of a sphere with radius at (x0,y0,z0) and executes func(i,j,k,radius) Exits loop when func(i,j,k,radius) return true. 



Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{Initializations_8h_source_l00261}{261}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{Initializations_8h_source}{Initializations.\+h}}.
